	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: ajax.php');
	writefile_1();
	if (!is_file('ajax.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): ajax.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('ajax.php') != '6e8a0d07058d123e2655b5319a8a8f23d63bf369') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): ajax.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('ajax.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of ajax.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('ajax.php') !== '6e8a0d07058d123e2655b5319a8a8f23d63bf369') {
		if (@sha1_file('ajax.php') !== '7f4897af39de46c945ffcfeff37ae2469193ecd9') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: ajax.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('ajax.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('ajax.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('ajax.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_1();
		if (@sha1_file('ajax.php') !== '6e8a0d07058d123e2655b5319a8a8f23d63bf369') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): ajax.php');
		}
	}
}

		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/publicPages/820_login_facebook/oauth.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/publicPages/820_login_facebook/oauth.php') != 'd27169cfd9563f0c92bf18e54017c1179348768c') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/publicPages/820_login_facebook/oauth.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/publicPages/820_login_facebook/oauth.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/publicPages/820_login_facebook/oauth.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/publicPages/820_login_facebook/oauth.php') !== 'd27169cfd9563f0c92bf18e54017c1179348768c') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/publicPages/820_login_facebook/oauth.php') !== '91ac88f0925bcaa33af6be8e8dfc13cc0c356d56') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/publicPages/820_login_facebook/oauth.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/publicPages/820_login_facebook/oauth.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/publicPages/820_login_facebook/oauth.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/publicPages/820_login_facebook/oauth.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_7();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/publicPages/820_login_facebook/oauth.php') !== 'd27169cfd9563f0c92bf18e54017c1179348768c') {

		}
